  <p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.090566s;">Privacy Policy</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.0962264s;">Effective as of Jan 1, 2021</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.101887s;">This Privacy Policy explains how we, Studio 369 inc handle information collected when you access this website, www.369.fun, and our related services, software, games, products, and content (collectively “Services”)</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.107547s;">By accessing any of our Services, you consent to our collection, storage, use and disclosure of your information as described in this Privacy Policy.  If you do not agree to any of the provisions of this Privacy Policy, you should not access or use this website or any of the Services. If you have any questions or concerns, you can contact us at privacy@369.fun</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.113208s;">This Privacy Policy only applies to our Services and is one portion of our Terms of Service, which governs your use of our Services.  You may find links to other websites, apps and services, or tools that enable you to share information with other websites, apps and services. We are not responsible for the privacy practices of these other websites, apps and services and we recommend that you review the privacy policies of each of these websites, apps or services before sharing any personal data.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.118868s;">Any disputes arising out of or relating to this Privacy Policy will be dealt with according to the dispute resolution procedures outlined in our Terms of Service accessible www.369.fun/tos</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.124528s;">Our Service is not intended for children. Anyone under the age of 13 is not permitted to access or use the Services and must not attempt to register an account or submit any personal information to us.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.130189s;">Table of Contents</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.135849s;">1. Categories of Information Collected</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.215094s;">1.1. Users may access certain elements of our Services, including the website, without need of registration.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.226415s;">1.1.2.  Payment Information. We and/or our third-party payment processor may collect and use payment information, such as credit card numbers and security codes, for the limited purpose of billing your account for in game purchases and other purchases made through the Services.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.232075s;">1.1.3. Information Relating to Your Voluntary Activities.  We may ask you to provide information in the context of the following activities on the Services:</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.237736s;">·                        Survey information:  If you participate in any survey, you will provide certain personal data as part of your response, unless you respond anonymously.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.243396s;">·                        Information that you post: You may provide personal data if you post comments, or contribute to community discussions</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.249057s;">·                        Information from correspondence: Information you send us (such as an email address or mobile phone number used to register or communicate with us), and referral information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.254717s;">·                        When use any of the forms on the Website, or contact us by mail, fax or other offline means.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.260377s;">1.2. Types of Non-Personal Information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.266038s;">1.2.1. Cookies and Tracking Technologies. We use standard tracking technologies like cookies, pixels and local storage, to collect certain types of non-personal information, including: (i) what web pages, apps and other Services you access; (ii) information about your mobile device (such as device and browser type); and (iii) your Internet protocol address, search query and other information.  </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.271698s;">We collect these types of information to help us provide you a more personalized and relevant online experience including by remembering your preferences, providing personalized content, and showing relevant ads.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.277358s;">1.2.2. Managing Cookies. Information about cookies is available at <a href="http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Faboutcookies.org%2F&amp;sa=D&amp;sntz=1&amp;usg=AFQjCNFIV3bec2lMZcB1KZPX2_OZ3-lSPQ" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline">http://aboutcookies.org</span></a>. Many web browsers allow you to manage your preferences. You can set your browser to refuse cookies or delete certain cookies. You may be able to manage other technologies in the same way that you manage cookies using your browser’s preferences. Please note that if you choose to block cookies, doing so may impair the Services or prevent certain elements of it from functioning.  </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.283019s;">Please note that even if you opt out using the mechanisms above, you may still receive advertisements when using the Services.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.288679s;">Because there is no accepted standard on how to respond to Do Not Track signals, we do not respond to such signals.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.29434s;">1.2.2. Information Collected By Third Parties.  We also acquire information from other trusted sources to update or supplement the information you provide or we collect automatically. If you access our Services from a third party service such as the Apple App Store, Google Play, Amazon App Store, or another third party site or service (“TPS”), you are subject to the privacy policies of the respective TPS.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.3s;">2.  Information Use</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.30566s;">We use personal and non-personal information collected for the following purposes:</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.311321s;">·         Create your accounts and allow access to our Services</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.316981s;">·         Provide technical support and respond to user inquiries</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.322642s;">·         Solicit input and feedback to improve our products and services and customize your user experience</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.328302s;">·         Inform users about new products, updates or promotional offers</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.333962s;">·         Customize your use of the Services and/or content or other material that we may send to you from time to time</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.339623s;">·         Engage in commonly accepted practices, such as contacting you at the email address we have on file if you are a potential winner in a sweepstakes or contest</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.345283s;">·         Improve and customize our Services and deliver and target advertising for example to show you interesting ads, when you visit third party websites. When you see our ads on a third-party website or apps, we or third-party services we engage for this purpose, may collect information your browser or mobile app makes available when seeing the ad (e.g. ip-addresses, referral URL, browser details, timestamp of request). Third party websites or apps may also allow us to measure the success of our ads on their websites. This may include e.g. whether a click converted to an actual purchase of a Subscription. Please see the privacy policy of such third-party websites to understand what data may be collected and how to opt-out. We may also show you ads on behalf of advertisers. We may use information that you make available to us when you interact with the Services, including location data, together with information you provide to us through the Services, e.g. demographic information, you choose to make available to us (such as your age or gender) directly or through third party services as well as information your browser sends us when using the Services (e.g. referral URLs, device type or location data).  This allows us to show you ads that are more relevant and interesting to you. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.350943s;">·         Prevent or take action against activities that are, or may be, in breach of our Terms of Use or applicable law.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.356604s;">·         For any other purpose, provided we disclose this to you at the relevant time, and provided that you agree to the proposed use of your personal data.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.362264s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.367925s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.373585s;">3. We use third-party vendors and hosting partners, for hardware, software, networking, storage, and related technology we need to run the Services, including the website.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.384906s;">If we merge with another company such that your information will become subject to a materially different privacy policy, we’ll notify you before the transfer. You can opt out of the new policy by deleting your account during the notice period.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.390566s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.396226s;">4. If you have an account, you can access and modify your personal information, or delete Please note that certain records will be retained for legal and accounting purposes.  To protect information from accidental or malicious destruction, we may not immediately delete residual copies from our active servers and may not remove information from our backup systems.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.407547s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.413208s;">5. If your TPS account is hacked, this may lead to unauthorized access, so be careful to keep your account information secure.  You use the Service at your own risk, and you’re responsible for taking reasonable measures to secure your account (like using a strong password).</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.435849s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.441509s;">6. We may also store such information on servers and equipment in other countries. You should be aware that privacy laws in the United States may not be equivalent to the laws in your country, and by using the Platform, you consent to the transfer, storage and processing of your personal data in the United States in accordance with this Privacy Policy and applicable law.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.45283s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.458491s;">7. If you are a California resident, you may make a request to us by email at privacy@369.fun Please include My California Privacy Rights in the subject line of your email and allow 30 days for us to respond. Because there is no accepted standard on how to respond to Do Not Track signals, we <span style="text-decoration:underline">do not</span> respond to such signals.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.469811s;"> </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.8s; transition-delay: 0.475472s;">8.
